LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[IsActive], [t].[LanguagesId], [t].[TV_ShowId], [t0].[Id] AS [Id0], [t0].[AttachmentId], [t0].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [t0].[Rating], [t0].[ReleaseDate], [t0].[Title], [t0].[URL]

) AS [t1] ON [l].[Id] = [t1].[LanguagesId]
